msg:Facilities: The facilities are not complete and there is no washing machine. It is a five-star hotel. Again, there is no greeter at the hotel entrance. The refrigerator in the room is yellow. The toilet seat is not placed on top of the toilet and is placed on the sink without looking carefully. Don't know at all
Hygiene: There is a question as to whether the cleaning is up to standard if the quilt in the room is itchy while sleeping.
Environment: Mainly because it is very close to Huangyan Beach. It is very convenient to go out and see the sea and play in the water opposite the hotel. If you need to book this hotel, you can come and take a look. You can't see the sunrise from the hotel. You can't see the sunset, you can only see a little bit of the sea. If you want to see the sunrise and sunset, you have to go to the beach. The sunrise is about 5.13 and the sunset is about 6.15. Pay attention to the time. The price/performance ratio is very low. Friends who want to see the sea are not Recommended choice
Service: There is no service. The staff are just hanging out. You have to go to the front desk to find them. They will not come over or ask you. Their tone is very cold and not enthusiastic at all. I spent five-star money to stay in a high-altitude sea view room and Itâ€™s the same as hotels outside, if you havenâ€™t already made a reservation, you wonâ€™t choose.

msg:The sanitation of the hotel is very poor. There is a strong smell when you enter the toilet. There is no exhaust fan switch. The hotel staff told you to turn on the toilet light and then turn on the exhaust system at the same time. I have doubts about this, because the air circulation is still poor, and the smell lingers for a long time . The table in the room was not wiped clean and there were stains. There were many thread ends on the towels in the bathroom. It felt like it had been recycled for a long time and was not replaced. The so-called luxury sea view is to look at a dilapidated terrace. After sleeping in this hotel for one night, I was bitten by insects a lot. It was unbearably itchy, not like mosquitoes. I doubted the cleanliness of bedding and carpets. The quality of the hotel is really bad, please book carefully.
